Even there are some simpler affiliate plaforms Impact helps me to control multiple partner accounts not only one. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">For me, discovering &amp; getting new affiliate partners could be better on Impact. Sometimes i got notifications but can not reach to provided partners. I think they should reconsider this process and they can offer more potential partners related to my actions.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">The second thing is I couldn't change my currency/bank account after i created my account. They want me to create another account but that's not easy if you want to get same partners to your board. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-5337702 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">I am able to control multiple partners on Impact without hassle. Daily action reminders, and snaphot widget is helpful. I can easily create deeplinks for any products of my partners. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link There are so many of them out there, it may seem impossible! But what you need is something that's simple, not too complicated or hard to understand, with decent program management and offers that you can be proud of promoting.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">That sums up Impact Radius very nicely. It's easy to use, you can easily select the most relevant offers for your demographic, and the program management is very helpful with matching up affiliates and merchants. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">It doesn't have quite as many offers as some competitors - but that's not a bad thing! The more offers there are out there, the more you have to compete with other affiliates for sign-ups. So, if your conversions are good enough, Impact Radius may be the perfect platform choice for you. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-5338850 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">We needed an affiliate platform that we could trust and one that would be easy to use. We wanted to build a broad network of affiliates, and we knew we'd need something simple to manage that. Impact Radius has all the features we need and then some. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f </p><p class="formatted-text">Oh, biggest problem with Impact is it doesn't let me stay logged in for any length of time - can you let publishers just stay logged in? <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4996959 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Hmm... one thing I love is when the affiliate program managers send me the complete URL with my affiliate code embedded, along with pics, so I can add Instagram and GETTR, too - maybe Pinterest? <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c
